–í–∞—Å–∏–ª–∏–π: –í—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ —Ä–µ—à–∏—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ—é –∑–∞–¥–∞—á—É —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–∞–º–∏.  –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –±—ç–∫, –∫–∞–∫ —É –≤–∞—Å —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å. –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –æ–Ω "–ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–≤–∞–ª" –∂–µ—Ç–æ–Ω—ã –∑–∞ —Ç–æ–Ω—ã. –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç, –¥–ª—è –Ω–µ–≥–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å jetton wallet, —Ç—É–¥–∞ —Å–º–∏–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç—å –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–π —Å–∞–ø–ª–∞–π –∂–µ—Ç–æ–Ω–æ–≤ –∏ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —ç—Ç–∏–º jetton –∫–æ—à–µ–ª—å–∫–æ–º —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ —ç—Ç–æ—Ç —Å–º–∞—Ä—Ç-–∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç, –ø—Ä–æ–¥–∞–≤–∞—è –∂–µ—Ç–æ–Ω—ã.  –†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–π –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏–¥—É–º–∞—Ç—å –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã—Ö.  –ü–æ–π–º–∏—Ç–µ, —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–æ–≤, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –Ω–∞–¥–æ –æ–±—è–∑–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–æ–±–ª—é–¥–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ—Ç. –í—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –≤–∑—è—Ç—å –ª—é–±–æ–π –∫–æ–¥ –∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ –∫–∞–∫ —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ, –∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥—è –∏–∑ –≤–∞—à–∏—Ö —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π. –ò —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –≤–∞—à DAPP –æ–Ω –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å.  –ù–æ –µ—Å–ª–∏ –≤—ã —Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –≤–∞—à –∫–æ–¥ "–≤—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª—Å—è" –≤ —ç–∫–æ—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—É, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã tonviewer —Ä–∞—Å–ø–æ–∑–Ω–∞–≤–∞–ª –≤–∞—à –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä –∏ jetton wallet –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –∫–∞–∫ minter –∏ jetton wallet, —Ç–æ –≤—ã –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –±—É–¥–µ—Ç–µ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å –ø—Ä–∏—Å—É—â–∏–π –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—É –∏ jetton wallet, –≤ —Ç–æ–º —á–∏—Å–ª–µ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–µ –≥–µ—Ç—Ç–µ—Ä—ã.  –Ø –Ω–µ–¥–∞–≤–Ω–æ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞–ª –∏–≥—Ä—É —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ minter –∏ jetton wallet. –ö–∞–∂–¥—ã–π –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π jetton wallet –±—ã–ª –∏ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–≤—ã–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–æ–º –∏–≥—Ä–æ–∫–∞, –≤ –Ω—ë–º —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –æ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–æ–º–æ–≤, –∞—Ä–º–∏–∏ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–∫–∞, —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∞ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–±–æ—Ä–∞ (–º–∏–Ω—Ç–∞) –º–æ–Ω–µ—Ç (–∂–µ—Ç–æ–Ω–æ–≤), —Å—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–π —Å –≥–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–æ–º. Minter –≤—ã—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞–ª –≥–ª–∞–≤–Ω—ã–º –∏–≥—Ä–æ–≤—ã–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–æ–º, —á–µ–∫–∞–Ω–∏–ª –º–æ–Ω–µ—Ç—ã –ø–æ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å—É –∏–≥—Ä–æ–∫–æ–≤, –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è–ª –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –ø–æ–∫—É–ø–∫–µ —Å–æ–ª–¥–∞—Ç, –≤—ã–ø–ª–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–ª —Ä–µ—Ñ–µ—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –≤–æ–∑–Ω–∞–≥—Ä–∞–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏—è. –Ø –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –≤–∑—è–ª –∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏–ª –≤ –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä –∏ jetton wallet —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –º–Ω–µ –±—ã–ª–æ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ –¥–ª—è –∏–≥—Ä—ã (–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ, –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ã, –≥–µ—Ç—Ç–µ—Ä—ã), –Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏–ª —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω—ã–µ –≥–µ—Ç—Ç–µ—Ä—ã. –ò –ø–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É –≤ tonviewer –º–æ–∏ —Å–º–∞—Ä—Ç –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç—ã –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è–ª–∏—Å—å –∫–∞–∫ minter –∏ jetton wallet.   –ü–æ –≤–∞—à–µ–º—É –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å—É, —è –±—ã —Å–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–ª —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –æ–ø–∫–æ–¥ –Ω–∞ –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ, –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª –±—ã –≤ sandbox, –∞ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª –±—ã –≤ mainnet. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ —Ö–æ—á–µ—Ç—Å—è –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä, —Ç–æ —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞ –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º –º–∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–∞, –∞ —Ç–∞–º —É–∂–µ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –≥–æ—Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –≤—Å—ë, —á—Ç–æ –∑–∞—Ö–æ—Ç–∏—Ç–µ. Zahar: def get_jetton_transfer_payload(sender_wallet_address: str, comment: str, amount: int = 25) -> str:         payload = (             begin_cell()             .store_uint(0xf8a7ea5, 32)             .store_uint(0, 64)             .store_coins(int(amount * 10 ** TWIF.JETTON_DECIMALS))             .store_address(AdminWallet.address) # –ê–¥—Ä–µ—Å—Å –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è             .store_address(sender_wallet_address) # –ê–¥—Ä–µ—Å—Å –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è             .store_maybe_ref(None)             .store_coins(int(0.02))             .store_maybe_ref(begin_cell().store_uint(0, 32).store_string(comment).end_cell())             .end_cell()             .to_boc()         )              return boc_to_base64_string(payload)   –≤—ã –±—ã –º–æ–≥–ª–∏ –º–Ω–µ –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –≤—ã–≥–ª—è–¥–µ—Ç—å –≤ –∏–¥–µ–∞–ª–µ, —è –Ω–µ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å —Å—Ç–ª–µ–Ω –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–π —Ç–µ–º–µ, –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ –∫–∞–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞–¥–æ —ç—Ç–æ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å (reply to 275077)

&rey: –Ø –∏–º–µ—é –≤ –≤–∏–¥—É def get_jetton_transfer_payload(sender_wallet_address: str, small_id: int, amount: int = 25) -> str:         payload = (             begin_cell()             .store_uint(0x0f8a7ea5, 32)             .store_uint(small_id, 64)             .....             .store_maybe_ref(None)             .store_coins(0)             .store_maybe_ref(None)             .end_cell()             .to_boc()         )              return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(payload)

Namon: () deploy_item(slice sender_address, int bid, cell item_code, slice cmd, slice full_domain, cell default_royalty_params) impure {     var (token_name, content, auction_config, royalty) = unpack_deploy_msg(cmd);     (slice beneficiary_address, int initial_min_bid, int max_bid, int min_bid_step, int min_extend_time, _) = unpack_auction_config(auction_config);     throw_unless(err::not_enough_funds, bid >= initial_min_bid);     int item_index = string_hash(token_name);      ... }  () recv_internal(int msg_value, cell in_msg_full, slice in_msg_body) impure {     ...      var (_, subwallet_id, public_key, _, item_code, full_domain, default_royalty_params) = unpack_collection_data();     var cmd = unwrap_signed_cmd(in_msg_body, public_key, subwallet_id, msg_value);     deploy_item(sender_address, msg_value, item_code, cmd, full_domain, default_royalty_params); } (reply to 276445)

SweetJesus: –Ω—É –≤ —Å–º—ã—Å–ª–µ –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å. –í –¥–æ–∫—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–Ω–∫–æ–Ω–Ω–µ–∫—Ç–∞ –µ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä—ã, –∫–∞–∫ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å. –£ —Ç–µ–±—è –µ—Å—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞, –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–π —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å –ø–æ–ª–µ payload, –≤ –Ω–µ–≥–æ –∑–∞–∫–∏–¥—ã–≤–∞–µ—à—å —è—á–µ–π–∫—É —ç—Ç—É –∏ —à–ª–µ—à—å. Namon: _ unwrap_signed_cmd(slice signed_cmd, int public_key, int subwallet_id, int msg_value) {     (slice signature, int hash, int got_subwallet_id, int valid_since, int valid_till, slice cmd)             = unpack_signed_cmd(signed_cmd);     throw_unless(err::invalid_signature, check_signature(hash, signature, public_key));     throw_unless(err::wrong_subwallet_id, subwallet_id == got_subwallet_id);     int ts = now();     throw_unless(err::not_yet_valid_signature, valid_since < ts);     throw_unless(err::expired_signature, ts < valid_till);     return cmd; }  (int, int, int, cell, cell, slice, cell) unpack_collection_data() inline {     var cs = get_data().begin_parse();     var res = (             cs~load_int(1), ;; touched             cs~load_uint(32), ;; subwallet_id             cs~load_uint(256), ;; owner_key             cs~load_ref(), ;; content             cs~load_ref(), ;; item_code             cs~load_text_ref(), ;; full_domain             cs~load_ref() ;; royalty_params     );     cs.end_parse();     return res; }  _ unpack_deploy_msg(slice cs) inline {     var res = (             cs~load_text(), ;; token_name             cs~load_ref(), ;; content             cs~load_ref(), ;; auction_config             cs~load_maybe_ref() ;; royalty     );     cs.end_parse();     return res; }  (slice, int, int, int, int, int) unpack_auction_config(cell c) inline {     slice cs = c.begin_parse();     var res = (             cs~load_msg_addr(), ;; beneficiary address             cs~load_grams(), ;; initial_min_bid             cs~load_grams(), ;; max_bid             cs~load_uint(8), ;; min_bid_step             cs~load_uint(32), ;; min_extend_time             cs~load_uint(32) ;; duration     );     cs.end_parse();     return res; } (reply to 276447)

message_to_estimate.serialize().to_boc().hex(),                     }                 ]             }         )          try:             seqno = await WalletV5R1.get_seqno(client, wallet.address)         except (Exception,):             seqno = 0          tether_transfer_for_send = wallet.create_signed_internal_msg(             messages=[                 wallet.create_wallet_internal_message(                     destination=Address(message.address),                     value=int(message.amount),                     body=Cell.one_from_boc(message.payload),                 ) for message in sign_raw_params.messages             ],             seqno=seqno,             valid_until=sign_raw_params.valid_until,         )          ext_message = wallet.create_external_msg(             dest=wallet.address,             body=tether_transfer_for_send,             state_init=wallet.state_init if seqno == 0 else None,         )          await api.gasless.send(             body={                 "wallet_public_key": wallet.public_key.hex(),                 "boc": ext_message.serialize().to_boc().hex(),             }         )          print(f"A gasless transfer sent!")         return True  –Ω–æ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ª–∏ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å usdt —á–µ–ª–æ–≤–µ–∫—É, –∞ –∫–æ–º–∏—Å—Å–∏—é –∑–∞–ø–ª–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å –Ω–µ –∑–∞ —Å—á–µ—Ç keeper battery

odnokasanie: –ö–æ–ª–ª–µ–≥–∏, –∫–∞–∫ —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é blueprint –∏–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∫—É –∏–∑ –∫–æ—à–µ–ª—å–∫–∞ –Ω–∞ –º–æ–π —Å–º–∞—Ä—Ç-–∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç usdt –∏–ª–∏ –ª—é–±–æ–≥–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–≥–æ jetton?  –ù–µ —Å–æ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∂—É —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –≤ —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç–µ —Å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º blueprint. –ù–∞–¥–æ –∂–µ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ - –Ω–∞–¥–æ –ª–∏ —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –æ–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–µ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –æ –ø—Ä–∏–µ–º–µ USDT jetton? –ú–Ω–µ –Ω–∞–¥–æ –∂–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∏—à–µ–ª –Ω—É–∂–Ω—ã–π –∂–µ—Ç–æ–Ω –∏ –¥–∞–ª—å–Ω–µ–π—à—É—é –±–∏–∑–Ω–µ—Å-–ª–æ–≥–∏–∫—É –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—Ç—å.

Timur: –ù–∞ —Å—á–µ—Ç –¥–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–∞, –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –µ—â–µ –æ–¥–∏–Ω —Å–º–∞—Ä—Ç –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω –∫–æ—à–µ–ª–µ–∫, –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ–ª—å—Ü–µ–º –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–∞–∫–æ–π —Ç–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç (–Ω–µ ¬´–æ–±—ã—á–Ω—ã–π¬ª–∫–æ—à–µ–ª–µ–∫) –∏ –≤ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–∞—Ö –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω –∫–æ—à–µ–ª—å–∫–æ–≤ –ø—Ä–∏ –ø–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω–æ–≤  –æ–Ω –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ-—É–≤–µ–¥–æ–º–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ–ª—å—Ü—É —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω –∫–æ—à–µ–ª—å–∫–∞ , –¥–∞–ª–µ–µ –≤–ª–∞–¥–µ–ª–µ—Ü –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç –ø—Ä–∏–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ —Å–æ–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏ –ø–æ—à–ª–æ-–ø–æ–µ—Ö–∞–ª–æ (–ª—é–±–∞—è –ª–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞ —Ç—ã—Ä—ã-–ø—ã—Ä—ã)  –ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ —Ç—ã –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—à—å —Å–≤–æ–∏ –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω—ã –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–º—É —á–µ–ª—É, —Ç—ã –Ω–µ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—à—å –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –≤ –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω –º–∞—Å—Ç–µ—Ä, —Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–æ–ª–æ–≥–∏—è —Ç–∞–∫–∞—è: –¢—ã -> ¬´–æ–±—ã—á–Ω—ã–π¬ª –∫–æ—à–µ–ª–µ–∫ —Ç–≤–æ–π -> –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω –∫–æ—à–µ–ª–µ–∫ —Ç–≤–æ–π -> –∂–µ—Ç—Ç–æ–Ω –∫–æ—à–µ–ª–µ–∫ —á–µ–ª–∞ (reply to 281588)

#: () deploy_user_contract(     int last_time_drop,      slice jetton_minter_address,      cell jetton_wallet_code,      int decimals,      cell user_drop_code,      int amount,      slice owner ) impure {     cell state_init = calculate_user_drop_state_init(last_time_drop, jetton_minter_address, jetton_wallet_code, decimals, user_drop_code);      var deploy_msg = begin_cell()         .store_uint(0x18, 6)                         .store_slice(user_drop_address)              .store_coins(70000000)                         .store_uint(4 + 2 + 1, 1 + 4 + 4 + 64 + 32 + 1 + 1 + 1)         .store_ref(state_init)                       .store_ref(             begin_cell()             .store_slice(owner)          .end_cell());      send_raw_message(deploy_msg.end_cell(), 1);      builder message = begin_cell()         .store_uint(0x18, 6)         .store_slice(smc_jetton_wallet_address)         .store_coins(62000000)         .store_uint(0, 1 + 4 + 4 + 64 + 32 + 1 + 1)         .store_uint(0xf8a7ea5, 32)         .store_uint(0, 64)         .store_coins(storage::to_claim)    ;; jettons_amount         .store_slice(user_drop_address)    ;; to_owner_address         .store_uint(0, 2)  ;; response_address (empty)         .store_int(0, 1)         .store_coins(30000000)         .store_int(0, 1)  ;; custom_payload (empty)         .store_ref(begin_cell()             .store_uint(op::send_jetton, 32)         .end_cell());         ;; .store_coins(0)   ;; forward amount to new_owner_address (null)         ;; .store_int(0, 1); ;; forward_payload (empty)          send_raw_message(message.end_cell(), 1);  }  if (~ storage::init?) { ;; one time for initialization address after deployment         throw_unless(405, equal_slices(storage::main_drop_address, sender_address));         storage::owner_address = in_msg_body~load_msg_addr();         save_data();          return ();           }      int op = in_msg_body~load_uint(32);      if (op == op::receive_jettons) {         storage::last_time_drop = cur_lt();         save_data();          slice smc_jetton_wallet_address = calculate_user_jetton_wallet_address(my_address(), storage::jetton_minter_address, storage::jetton_wallet_code);         throw_unless(403, equal_slices(sender_address, smc_jetton_wallet_address)); ;; check jetton wallet          int query_id = in_msg_body~load_uint(64);         int msg_jetton_amount = in_msg_body~load_coins();         throw_unless(104, msg_jetton_amount > 0);         slice from_address = in_msg_body~load_msg_addr();         in_msg_body~skip_bits(1);          slice inner_payload = in_msg_body~load_ref().begin_parse();         int inner_op = inner_payload~load_uint(32);         throw_unless(105, inner_op == op::send_jetton);          if (inner_op == op::send_jetton) {             msg::send_simple_jettons(smc_jetton_wallet_address, storage::owner_address, msg_jetton_amount, 52000000, 1, 0);             return ();         }      }
